He was in and out in 20 minutes both times before, this time I was asked to come back in an hour and a half when he woke up. This seemed odd, so I asked to speak with the doctor again to clarify. < text>
Our dog got hurt on a Sunday and he needed to be seen ASAP. I thought his leg might be broken. Our usual vet, Abby Pet, is closed on Sundays. I drove him to Family Pet Hospital, the nearest emergency clinic. Due to COVID, the clinic is not taking walk-ins, but when I called the number posted on the door they agreed to see us. Within less than two hours from pulling in, we had seen the Dr who did a thorough physical exam, and recommended a course of action (he opined it was most likely sprained, not broken). Our pup got a pain shot and some meds for the week and we were on our way. The total was presented to me before any treatment was administered. Now, the Vet could have stated xrays were necessary and I would have paid for them, but he was ethical and did not recommend them based on the physical exam. Overall I found this facility to be responsive, compassionate and fair. Highly recommend!!!< /text>

<UserId.>103318249408244557080</UserId.>< Review>
We have been going to Family Pet for 10 years.  We breed Golden Retrievers and it has been a tough week with our pack. We lost one of our dogs to liver failure and we welcomed a new litter with serious complications at the delivery. I feel like I have been living at Family Pet.

To say that Dr. Gil & Dr. Singh are extraordinary is an understatement. Not only do they love the dogs, but they are exceptional practitioners. They are holistic in their approach, assessing systems and evaluating what all the pieces of information mean. And yet, they are cautious with testing so as not to bankrupt their client in the process. I appreciate the balanced approach and have often been amazed by how reasonable my bill is when all is said and done. But most importantly, amazed by the way they've been able to discern an underlying cause and help our Goldens recover. We've been through it all with them: cancer, c-sections, liver failure, dog fights, heart worms (put your dogs on meds!), pyometra, and even a dog who got electrocuted by chewing a fan cord. They have treated it all with incredible skill and kindness.

The vet techs are just as fabulous, as they really LOVE their jobs and are super knowledgeable. I just can't speak highly enough of the docs and staff at Family Pet. If I could give more than 5 stars, I would...</Review>

WARNING:

< Review>
I have fostered many cats and have had many experiences with vets before but this was the worst vet experience I have ever had.

We brought in my cat twice for different reasons. The second time we took our cat in, he was not doing too well. The vet didn't really address our concern and jumped to conclusions. We were told an ultrasound would confirm if our cat had bladder stones or crystals, so we stuck for an ultrasound. The vet couldn't see anything because there was no urine in his bladder. The vet recommend a UA test but we didn't know the cost or didn't know anything about the UA because we were never informed. The vet assured us that we can still see stones in the bladder on a ultrasound so we asked for just an ultrasound. We were asked to bring our cat in the following day for him to collect more urine. We come back the next morning and the vet and vet tech push and push for us to do the UA test with still no information. The vet does the ultrasound and still doesn't see anything because there was no urine. We were asked to leave our cat until later that day so that there would be urine in his bladder. We agree but decline the UA several times. We come back hours later to pick up our cat and there is a charge on our bill for the UA. They did the UA without our consent. When we complain to the vet tech that helped the vet with the procedure, she was completely unprofessional and rude. She was sighing and raising her voice at us. She told us that because we didn't sign a decline form, they proceeded. When we asked for the vet, he said we verbally consented to the UA and that it was in the plan all along. We were still charged for the UA and proceeded to send the results to the UA since the procedure was already done without our consent. When the lab tech called us with the results, we were told that there was no documentation of anything on our cat and they had no idea why the UA was done in the first place. This vet office is so unorganized and so unprofessional. We have paid hundreds of dollars for their care and this is how they treated us. The vet called to apologize but we are too afraid to bring our cat back again.

Please do not ever bring your fur babies here! I would hate for them to get the same treatment or worse. Steer clear!!<//Review>

< Text>
+2 stars for helping my dog somewhat, long open hours, and really great that they email you any lab results on your dog and give you access to a vet app for your dog that shows what they did.

However, -3 stars for everything else. They function similar to an ER for pets. Open long hours, and charging very expensive fees. On my first visit for my dog, they did not greet me so I had to ask if I needed to sign in. They said go ahead. They gave me a registration form to fill out. After I gave it back to them, I had to wait over 25 minutes to just go into a room. I made an appt beforehand too, but still had to wait a long time. There was also no one else waiting in the lobby when I was there.

The lobby is very dim and low lit, not welcoming at all. Even during the day, the lobby is very gloomy and dark. Even worse, when I was sitting there, I could overhear the receptionists talking to a disgruntled customer on the phone about the fees for their dog who just had surgery that day. From what I heard, the vet had to do ‚Äúextra‚Äù and necessary things once they opened up her dog in surgery, so that‚Äôs why it was more than the estimate. The vet even came out and looked angry when telling the receptionists what to say to the customer on the phone about the fees. It was over $2000+, so it‚Äôs obvious why the customer was not happy. I heard all of this when I was sitting there for my appointment.

After being seen by the vet (who has a thick accent that was hard to understand), the vet seemed extremely motivated and pushed a lot for doing surgery for my dog. He said it would be in the upward range of $1500+. He also did not give me any other options but surgery. I wanted to wait for more tests, and see if my dog would get better, not really knowing what the results really meant. The vet kept pressuring me to do the surgery or my dog would die. After discussing with my family, we decided to wait on the surgery. Before we left, I had to pay more than what they had estimated. It was over $800, when they gave me an estimate around $600. They added things without my knowledge, and it was not even surgery. Just extra antibiotic injections. They never told me about extra shots.

We went the next day for more tests to see if my dog was getting better. Tests came back with my dog a little bit better but still in very bad condition. When the vet realized that we were not going to do surgery and still wait longer, he left the room abruptly and angry. I never saw him again. I still had some questions to ask him, so I just asked the receptionist. She answered them and then she checked me out after paying again, this time only $100+ for some more injections.

The worst thing is that I asked 4-5 times for the actual estimated cost for the surgery, so we could better decide to do it or not. They refused to tell me every time. I asked the vet and receptionists. This is why we didn‚Äôt do it too, because it was probably going to be very expensive. I don‚Äôt think they tell you until you say YES to the surgery. It would be hard to say NO after committing to it already.

The next couple days, I went to my regular vet and they did more tests. Based on the results, they said there was no way they would have operated on such bad blood results. My dog may have died from blood loss on the surgery table if they operated over the weekend. Also, the surgery at my regular vet was only around $600, including meds and a cone. It was going to be much more expensive at Family Pet Hospital. I‚Äôm sure it would have been in the $2000+ range. I‚Äôm so glad we waited. My dog survived and is well now.

Overall, do not go here if you have a more reliable, friendly, and less expensive vet. Only go here if you have no other choice. Don‚Äôt go for checkups or surgery. They overcharge here and will add things onto your bill without your knowledge and still expect you to pay. This place would be a good alternative to the ER, but prices are still very expensive here.< /Text>

<user_name>DBL.G.</user_name><userid>109668874662539536710<//userid>< text>
Legg Lake is a very big park, has plenty of picnic tables & is great to have a BBQ with family and friends.
This park has large lakes with plenty of wild life that live in the lakes, you can fish here as long you carry your fishing license. They stock the lakes here @ Legg Lake with Carp & Catfish & several other fishes. This park has plenty of parking.. the bathrooms are at maintained daily & there's vendors that sell ice cream & fresh fruit.. a great place to bring the kids. Lots of ducks & Geese that roam around throughout this park.. some of the geese are very aggressive @ times & they will come at you ..so when you bring the little ones (kids) keep an eye on them cus they do go after them especially if they are eating a snack.
You can ride bikes ,do some jogging or go for a walk with your pet dog.
Located on Rosemead Blvd in S.El Monte.<//text>

< review>
0 stars (apparently, you must choose between 1~5 stars for this to register). I was seriously considering buying one of these massage chairs (had narrowed it down to this, Osaki, Kahuna), but when I took a good look at the reviews, I found that there was something strange about them (both on Amazon and Google).  If you look at the review postings by members who have posted reviews of multiple products/businesses, you will indeed find strange patterns.  For example, there is an unusually high number of head lice clinics in the Los Angeles area, all with workers there named Amy and Patty (4 different head lice clinics in the LA area reviewed by a single member, among others), an abundance of garage door companies in the Texas area, etc.

Now, I don't know whether this is a good product or not, but these posts do not inspire confidence.  If it is indeed a good product, then why not let the quality speak for itself?  I'm going with the Osaki, a brand that is frequently stocked by Costco.< /review>

< Review>
Small dining area, has 5 tables that seat 4, 2 tables that can accomodate 6, and a long bar that can seat singles and doubles. Food here is fantastic, I have been here twice, and both times the service was prompt and courteous. I recommend the KB fries for some delicious karaage and bulgogi. Also, the cold ramen with sesamr dressinf has a lovely flavor and is great if you need a cool entree. The takoyaki is great, it's served very hot (temperature-wise) and comes with all the proper sauce and bonito flakes. Karaage is also good, tender, juicy meat with a crisp exterior for a nice crunch.<//Review>

‚Äî
+ Dill Chicken Sandwich: BOMB. So much texture and flavor thanks to the crispy chicken, fresh veggies and dill sauce. I loved the herby infusion from the dill, not too common! Eyeing the truffle sandwich next.

+ 1/2 Chicken N Chips Meal: Their rotisserie is so flavorful and I couldn‚Äôt stop munching on the seasoned fries. I‚Äôm a dark meat gal so you know that was my favorite part!

+ Chicken N Chips Wrap: yes, you can get your meal as a wrap! The combo of roasted chicken, potatoes, stuffing, and gravy literally tastes like Thanksgiving in a burrito.

‚Äî

< Review>
The only positive thing I can say about their chicken sandwiches is that they're healthier than fried chicken sandwiches. Other than that, the food is mediocre.

I got the spicy chicken sandwich. It wasn't spicy AT ALL. In fact, it was pretty bland. The chicken was also dry; not terribly dry, but dry enough. The fries were also soggy (this is the case with most take-out places I've gotten fries from - they use containers which trap the heat, thereby producing moisture which makes the fries soggy. Why can't places use materials that absorb the moisture!?)

The food wasn't terrible but there are better places to go.</Review>

<rate>5</rate>< Review>
Luckily, I found this place through grubhub's local search. I had the truffle chicken sandwich and the small chips. I can say without a doubt that it was the best rotisserie chicken sandwich I've ever had! The chicken was tender and there was the perfect amount of lettuce, tomato, and truffle aioli. Another thing I really enjoyed about this sandwich was the brioche bun. It had a little sweetness and was just the right amount of thin. I don't care for sandwiches with large buns that I feel like I'm mostly getting full on the large amount of bread. The chips were also great and so was the ice tea. Chicken N Chips will definitely be a "go to" sandwich spot for me!</Review>

< name>
Torrey Carlson</name>
<date>1495136703158<//date><Rating>3<//Rating>< review>
Considering all the amazing coffee house options on Long Beach, I'm not super impressed. The coffee was good and it has a decent atmosphere, but the service was not great. The barista was rude and unwelcoming. Also, it's pretty obvious the owner takes the cheap route on things. There is a difference between "vintage" and "old" - vintage is cool, chic, and eclectic; old is outdated, dirty, and falling apart. Unfortunately, their furniture and decor is not vintage, just old. The coffee table I was sitting near was being held together by electrical tape, the picture in the bathroom has 2 holes in it and looks like they got it at a garage sale and hung it up without cleaning it, and what's with the cheap styrofoam cups? I'm paying $5 for coffee and I can't get a mug, or even a nice sturdy cup? Just seems cheap and not very eco-conscious. Anyway, still have it 3 stars for the good coffee, the fact that they're open late, and I can see what they're trying to do. It's not BAD, and if there were no better options in town I'd probably keep coming here, but Long Beach has no shortage of amazing coffee shops so I probably won't be back. They need to step up their game - they've got a lot of competition!< /review>
